<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause to hang, to hang</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang somewhere else</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang someone (to execute by hanging)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang oneself (to commit suicide by hanging)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verheffing.html>verheffing</a> (78527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verheffinge</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhelderen.html>verhelderen</a> (50412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helder.html>helder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhelderen.html>verhelderen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to clarify, elucidate, illuminate</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:verhelderen.html>verhelderen</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verhuegen</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhoging.html>verhoging</a> (16445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verhogine</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhogen.html>verhogen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhoging.html>verhoging</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhogingen.html>verhogingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhoging.html>verhoginkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>increase, the act of raising</li>
<li>elevation, an eminence <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">raised portion of <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>elevated body <a href = vnd.unilang:temperaturen.html>temperature</a>, mild fever, febrile hyperthermia</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">verhouden</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>, often considered a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Verhältnis</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>proportion

***verhuiswagen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhuiswagen.html>verhuiswagen</a> (52891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhuizen.html>verhuizen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wagen.html>wagen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhuiswagen.html>verhuiswagen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhuiswagens.html>verhuiswagens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhuiswagen.html>verhuiswagentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A removal <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>, a moving <a href = vnd.unilang:truck.html>truck</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
